### [155] [NAVIRA: Decoupled Stochastic Remasking for Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06031)
*Andrey Fomenko,Maksim Kryzhanovskiy,Svetlana Glazyrina,Roman Ischenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种改进的掩码扩散语言模型解码策略，通过解耦评分和再掩码过程，提高了文本生成的流畅性和多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有掩码扩散语言模型为提升生成速度，会并行预测多个token，但这导致早期局部错误会污染后续上下文，在生成质量上存在缺陷。已有方法如PRISM通过学习质量分数并重掩码低质量token进行纠正，但推理过程中解码与掩盖耦合，导致错误信息依然影响后续生成。

Method: 提出NAVIRA推理解码策略，将token评分与掩盖位置选择过程分离。首先做一次前向传播评估token质量，选定低质量token进行再掩码，然后进行第二轮前向传播，在清理后的上下文中重新生成被掩码的token。此外使用温度控制的随机掩码机制，减少对同一位置重复修正并平衡流畅性和多样性。

Result: 在170M参数规模的掩码扩散语言模型实验中，解耦后的解码策略有效提升了文本的流畅度，有计划的随机再掩码机制则在多轮预测下保持更高的熵，并在LLM-judge评分下表现更优。实验显示解码时的再掩码策略比单纯依赖学习的质量信号更关键。

Conclusion: 再掩码策略对于可靠的掩码扩散文本生成至关重要，提出的NAVIRA方法在准确性与生成多样性方面均有显著改进，为未来高质量高效率文本生成提供了新路径。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models generate text by iteratively unmasking many tokens in parallel, but this speed comes with a correction problem: tokens generated in the same step are predicted from marginal distributions, and early local dependency errors can later contaminate the context. PRISM addresses this by learning token-level quality scores and remasking unreliable tokens, but its inference rule is coupled: the same forward pass both detects low-quality tokens and computes logits for their replacements, so the erroneous tokens still condition regeneration. We propose NAVIRA, an inference-time decoding policy that separates these two operations and samples remasking positions stochastically. A first forward pass scores tokens; selected tokens are masked; a second forward pass regenerates from the cleaned context. Temperature-controlled remasking reduces repeated correction of the same positions and balances fluency against diversity. In controlled experiments with a 170M masked diffusion language model, decoupling improves fluency, while scheduled stochastic remasking preserves entropy and achieves stronger LLM-judge scores under larger forward-pass budgets. These results show that remasking policy, not only the learned quality signal, is central to reliable masked-diffusion text generation.

</details>


### [156] [IA-RAG: Interval-Algebra-Driven Temporal Reasoning for Dynamic Knowledge Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06044)
*Xiaoman Wang,Yaoze Zhang,Wenzhuo Fan,Hongwei Zhang,Ding Wang,Guohang Yan,Song Mao,Botian Shi,Yunshi Lan,Pinlong Cai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对时序知识的RAG框架（IA-RAG），通过时间区间和层次化的方法增强大模型的时序推理与检索能力，显著提升了复杂时序问答任务的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG及其图结构扩展版本仅将知识当作静态信息，或仅用粗粒度时间戳，难以捕捉丰富的时序结构（如持续、重叠、包含等），这限制了模型对复杂时间关系的理解与推理能力。

Method: 提出IA-RAG框架：1) 将事实建模为区间事件单元（IEU）；2) 以主题森林（Thematic Forest）层次结构管理IEU，节点间基于Allen区间代数表达时序依赖；3) 在时间边界不完整或模糊时，引入子图时间收紧机制，通过逻辑约束细化区间；4) 检索时利用区间代数指导的遍历实现隐式时序语义检索。

Result: 在TimeQA、TempReason、ComplexTR等多个时序问答基准上，IA-RAG在时序检索和复杂组合时序推理任务中取得了领先的表现。

Conclusion: IA-RAG能显式、高效地对知识的时序结构建模，在复杂时序推理任务上具有明显优势，并为RAG类模型引入精细时序推理能力奠定了基础。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has shown strong effectiveness in grounding Large Language Models (LLMs) with external knowledge. However, existing RAG and Graph RAG frameworks largely treat knowledge as static or associate time with coarse-grained timestamps or metadata, failing to capture rich temporal structures such as duration, overlap, and containment. We propose IA-RAG, a hierarchical temporal RAG framework that models knowledge as time intervals and performs retrieval under formal temporal constraints. IA-RAG represents facts as Interval Event Units (IEUs) and organizes them into a hierarchical Thematic Forest, where temporal dependencies are governed by Allen's Interval Algebra. To handle incomplete or uncertain temporal boundaries, IA-RAG further introduces a Sub-graph Time Tightening mechanism that refines fuzzy intervals through logical constraints within connected event subgraphs. In addition, IA-RAG supports implicit temporal semantic retrieval through interval-algebra-guided traversal. Experiments on multiple temporal question answering benchmarks, including TimeQA, TempReason, and ComplexTR, demonstrate that IA-RAG achieves strong temporal retrieval and reasoning performance, particularly on complex compositional temporal reasoning tasks. Our code is released at https://github.com/xiaoAugenstern/LogicalRAG_TemporalQA.

Our results show that text-only XCOMET and multimodal LLM Qwen2.5-Omni are able to perform the STEL task in roughly half the precision of humans. We also find that direct speech processing is necessary for the STEL task, and that the current text-only and speech-processing systems are complementary in labelling translation-only vs. speech-processing errors in ST.

*Seung Hwan Cho,Young-Min Kim*

Result: MTL能提升意图语义的表现，但英语任务下表层转录性能下降且随表层-语义分歧加剧。分析显示，韩语编码器能区分两项任务，英语却高度耦合，导致表层转录受损。

Conclusion: 建议未来的MTL设计应关注减缓编码器层面的任务纠缠，减少在双输出L2语音识别中的表层退化问题。

Abstract: Second-language (L2) speech recognition often requires transcriptions of pronunciations and intended meanings. Multi-task learning (MTL) is a natural approach because it assumes that shared representations benefit both outputs. However, this paper shows that this assumption does not hold across Korean and English. MTL improves meaning but degrades surface transcription, especially in English, where the degradation scales with surface-meaning divergence measured by Levenshtein edit distance.Encoder analysis links these patterns to encoder-level entanglement, with Korean preserving distinct task representations while English produces nearly identical ones. Cross-task decoder analysis shows that the meaning dual-output decoder adapts with a unique representation, while the surface dual-output decoder remains constrained by the encoder. These findings motivate the design of MTL frameworks that mitigate encoder-level entanglement to reduce surface degradation in dual-output L2 automatic speech recognition.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SkillComposer将技能构建分解为创建、改进、合并三种可学习的操作，并通过系统性拒绝采样训练，使语言模型在推理时自我进化；支持离线、在线、混合三种部署模式来满足不同需求。

Abstract: Agent skills, which consist of reusable strategies that guide agent reasoning and action, have shown strong potential for improving model capability at inference time. However, current skill construction methods treat the problem as one-shot extraction, overlooking a fundamental tension: a skill tailored to the specific task fails to transfer, while the abstracted skill often provides insufficient guidance. We attribute this fragility to the absence of explicit mechanisms for skill specification and generalization. To address this gap, we introduce SkillComposer, a framework that decomposes skill construction into three learnable operations: create, improve, and merge. Trained via systematic rejection sampling recipe, SkillComposer enables language models to self-evolve skills at inference time and supports three deployment modes: offline for building generalized libraries, online for task-specific refinement, and hybrid for combining both. Comprehensive experiments on $τ^2$-Bench, LiveCodeBench v6, and AppWorld show that SkillComposer consistently outperforms baselines. Our SkillComposer-4B improves a 27B executor by up to +4.5 on agent tasks and +3.4 on code tasks, while generalizing across domains and task types unseen during training. Analysis reveals that merge and improve address orthogonal quality dimensions and that skill composition is a transferable meta-ability, providing a practical recipe for skill-augmented inference.

### [160] [LatentSkill: From In-Context Textual Skills to In-Weight Latent Skills for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06087)
*Aofan Yu,Chenyu Zhou,Tianyi Xu,Zihan Guo,Rong Shan,Zhihui Fu,Jun Wang,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang,Jianghao Lin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Agent系统在每一步都需要将技能文本注入prompt中，导致上下文开销大且技能内容被明文暴露，缺乏高效且安全的技能复用机制。

Method: 该方法通过预训练超网络，将文本技能转化为可插拔的LoRA适配器（LoRA adapter），并将技能存储在参数空间（weight space）而非上下文空间。实现技能模块的加载、扩展与组合，消除per-step技能token，提升系统效率和安全性。

Result: 在ALFWorld和Search-QA两项任务中，LatentSkill的表现均优于传统的in-context技能方法，且大幅减少了技能token的使用。例如，在ALFWorld的seen/unseen分割上分别提升了21.4和13.4分，预填充token减少64.1%；在Search-QA上精确匹配率提升3.0分，技能token开销减少72.2%。

Conclusion: LatentSkill展示了权重空间存储技能的有效性与高效性，具备模块化、可伸缩、低暴露等优势，是LLM Agent系统技能扩展的理想底层机制。

Abstract: Agent systems increasingly use textual skills to encode reusable task procedures, but injecting these skills into the prompt at every step incurs substantial context overhead and exposes skill content as plaintext. We present LatentSkill, a framework that converts textual skills into plug-and-play LoRA adapters through a pretrained hypernetwork. LatentSkill stores skill knowledge in weight space rather than context space, removing per-step skill tokens while preserving modular loading, scaling, and composition. On ALFWorld and Search-QA, LatentSkill outperforms the corresponding in-context skill baseline while using substantially fewer prefill tokens: it improves ALFWorld success by 21.4 and 13.4 points on the seen and unseen splits with 64.1% fewer prefill tokens, and improves Search-QA exact match by 3.0 points with 72.2% lower skill-token overhead. Further analysis shows that generated skill LoRAs form a structured semantic geometry, can be precisely controlled via the LoRA scaling coefficient, and can be composed through parameter-space arithmetic when skill components are aligned. These findings suggest that weight-space skills provide an efficient, modular, and less exposed substrate for extending LLM agents.

However, it still underuses structural context in two places: cross-KG interaction is weak during encoding, and final candidate ranking still relies too heavily on coarse similarity. We address these limitations with ContextEA, an enhanced encoder-decoder framework for transferable EA. Method: 作者设计了Ouvia评估框架，专注一对一英语到葡萄牙语对话的语音翻译场景，涵盖医疗和日常情境，通过定制Web应用与多阶段研究，收集了超过1750次实际交互，涉及3种英语口音和2种性别，多种ST系统，综合分析可用性的用户评估。

Result: 现代语音翻译系统的实际可用性有限，只有大约一半对话被认为可用；不同性别和方言用户的可用性评分存在显著差异。另外，基于问答（QA）的方法比传统指标更能预测现实中的可用性。

Conclusion: 应重视以用户为中心的、情境化的评估体系，而不应只依赖整体质量分数。未来的ST系统应关注技术能为哪些用户群体提供高质量服务以及如何提升其实际交流可用性。

Abstract: Speech translation (ST) is increasingly adopted in user applications, yet its evaluation largely focuses on decontextualized testbeds and holistic quality, rather than end users' communication needs. We introduce Ouvia, an evaluation framework for measuring user-perceived usability of speech translation outputs in real-world settings. Ouvia focuses on one-to-one communication: an English speaker needs to convey a request to a Portuguese speaker, and the message is automatically translated. Through a custom web app and multi-phase study design, we collect more than 1,750 such interactions in healthcare and everyday situations, mediated by four ST systems, involving speakers from three English dialects and two genders. We find that modern ST serves people only to a limited extent -- only around half of interactions are rated as usable -- with significant gaps in reported usability across demographic groups. Moreover, among quality metrics, we find that QA-based evaluation is a substantially stronger predictor of real-world usability than standard approaches. Together, these findings stress the importance of situated, user-centered evaluation frameworks that go beyond holistic quality scores and attend to who the technology serves -- and how well.

</details>


### [165] [The Tell-Tale Norm: $\ell_2$ Magnitude as a Signal for Reasoning Dynamics in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06188)
*Jinyang Zhang,Hongxin Ding,Yue Fang,Weibin Liao,Muyang Ye,Junfeng Zhao,Yasha Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出，LLM中隐状态的L2范数可以作为其层间推理强度的内生信号，并通过稀疏自编码器诊断和理论推导，验证该信号能够指示模型推理的关键时刻。基于此，设计了三种无需额外训练的基于L2范数的推理增强技术，显著提升推理表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然众多研究关注于理解LLM中的推理机制，但仍缺乏用于描述推理动态的原生且有理论依据的层内信号。本文试图寻找一种本征信号，能直观反映模型各层推理强度及动态变化，从而更好地分析和增强大模型推理能力。

Method: 作者利用稀疏自编码器（SAEs）对LLM各层隐状态进行分析，发现隐状态L2范数在推理特征被激活时显著上升。他们进一步通过理论证明L2范数可以界定SAE推理特征的激活强度，并通过实证相关分析及因果干预，确认L2范数能忠实反映关键推理时刻。最后设计了三种推理增强技术，均基于L2范数信号，不需额外训练或数据。

Result: 实验证明L2范数显著与推理步骤相关，基于此开发的三种技术（层间递归、状态引导、响应选择）在不同架构及推理基准上均带来显著推理性能提升。

Conclusion: L2范数为理解与操控LLM潜在推理动态提供了可靠、简单的途径，相关技术可提升推理表现，对大模型推理研究和应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Recent work has sought to understand Large Language Models (LLMs) reasoning, yet a principled, model-intrinsic signal that captures its layer-wise reasoning dynamics remains underexplored. We bridge this gap by demonstrating that the l2 norm of hidden states serves as an endogenous signal of the model's reasoning intensity. Using Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) as a diagnostic probe, we observe that LLMs' internal reasoning is marked by a sharp increase in reasoning feature activations concentrated in late layers. Motivated by this pattern, we establish a formal link between reasoning intensity and the model's latent geometry and theoretically prove that the l2 norm of hidden states bounds the activation strength of SAE reasoning features. Empirical correlation analysis and causal interventions further validate the l2 norm as a faithful indicator, where heightened norms consistently correspond to critical reasoning steps. We then introduce three test-time scaling techniques guided by l2 norms: (i) Adaptive Layer-wise Reasoning Recursion, (ii) Endogenous Reasoning State Steering, and (iii) l2-guided Response Selection, which requires no additional training or data and is compatible with advanced inference engines. Experiments across model architectures and benchmarks show that l2-norm-based techniques significantly improve reasoning performance, offering a principled yet simple lens to perceive and control LLM latent reasoning dynamics. Our code is available at https://github.com/zjy1298/The-Tell-Tale-Norm.

</details>

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过对大型语言模型（以Roberta-base为例）进行微调，提高基于上下文的问题回答系统的准确率和相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用SQuAD1.1数据集，对预训练大语言模型（如Roberta-base）进行有监督微调，提升其对上下文的理解和答案抽取能力。

In this work, we propose a question answering system based on large language models, where the input consists of a textual context and a corresponding question, and the output is a concise and accurate answer. The motivation behind this research lies in addressing the limitations of current QA systems, particularly their tendency to produce irrelevant or imprecise responses despite having access to the correct context. Our methodology involves fine-tuning a pre-trained LLM on a benchmark QA dataset to improve its contextual comprehension and answer extraction capabilities. Specifically, we utilize the Stanford Question Answering Dataset (SQuAD1.1), which provides high-quality context-question-answer triplets for supervised training and evaluation. These results indicate strong accuracy and answer relevance, demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed approach for context-based question answering tasks. ### [167] [Dense Contexts Are Hard Contexts: Lexical Density Limits Effective Context in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06203)
*Giovanni Dettori,Matteo Boffa,Danilo Giordano,Idilio Drago,Marco Mellia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文发现，除了输入长度和关键信息位置，词汇密度也是影响大模型长上下文性能的重要因素，词汇密度高会显著降低模型有效上下文窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究多关注输入长度和信息位置对于长上下文表现的影响，而词汇密度这一因素很少被系统研究。实际应用中，很多输入文本信息密集，因此亟需系统评估词汇密度对模型效果的影响。

Method: 作者设计了三个“针/大海捞针”类基准测试，控制上下文长度（一致为约12k tokens）和目标信息位置，仅调整文本信息的密度。实验对9B-685B参数规模的开源大模型，观察其在不同密度下的信息检索能力，并通过多种设置排除任务类型干扰。

Result: 发现随着词汇密度的提升，模型性能（信息检索得分）显著下降：原本在稀疏信息下能近乎完美检索，在高密度文本中得分低于60%。而降低密度则明显恢复性能。

Conclusion: 词汇密度直接影响大模型的有效上下文容量。在处理信息密集型输入时，需关注词汇密度对LLM性能的压缩作用，对实际系统设计和应用有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Input length and the position of relevant information are widely cited as the primary causes of degraded LLM long-context performance. Here, we study lexical density -- the rate at which a context introduces distinct information -- as a third, largely overlooked factor that systematically reduces the effective context window of LLMs. We quantify the impact of lexical density on open-weight LLMs (9B-685B) using three "find-the-needle" style benchmarks with identical length (~12k tokens) and controlled needle position, but increasing density of information. We observe a sharp performance collapse in higher-density benchmarks: models that are near-perfect in sparse contexts drop below 60% retrieval score on denser ones. To rule out task-type confounds, we vary and control the density within each benchmark while keeping all other properties unchanged. Reducing density generally restores performance, especially in the high-density regimes where degradation appears. These results show that effective context capacity is a function of lexical density, with direct implications for real-world LLM systems operating on compact, information-rich inputs.

Method: 作者构建了一个涵盖人道报告、世行政策文件等多种类别的基准数据集，并对其中含有可复用分析信息的图表做了标注。用此数据集评测了多个开源文档版面检测模型，从检测准确性与空间定位等多方面进行比较分析。

In this work, we introduce a benchmark dataset and evaluation framework for \textit{data snapshot extraction}, the task of identifying and localizing semantically meaningful visual artifacts within institutional documents. The benchmark spans humanitarian reports, World Bank policy research working papers, and project appraisal documents, and includes annotations for figures and tables that contain reusable analytical information. Using this dataset, we benchmarked multiple open-source layout detection models and evaluated both detection performance and spatial extraction quality. Our results show that current models struggle to generalize to operational institutional documents despite strong performance on conventional academic benchmarks. Common failure modes include confusion between analytical and non-analytical content, fragmentation of composite analytical artifacts, and incomplete extraction of contextual information required for interpretation. These findings highlight a persistent gap between generic document layout analysis and operationally useful data snapshot extraction. We release the source PDFs, annotation dataset, metadata, and source code to support future research in operational document intelligence. ### [170] [From Self to Other: Evaluating Demographic Perspective-Taking in LLM Hate Speech Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06266)
*Paloma Piot,Javier Parapar*

TL;DR: 本论文研究了用个性化大型语言模型（Persona-conditioned LLMs）来模拟不同群体对仇恨言论标注的分歧，发现模型难以全面还原人类间的主观差异，但特定设置下能够较好地近似人类分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仇恨言论的判定高度主观，不同群体的感知标准差异很大，手工采集多群体标注成本高、难以扩展。借助具备特定身份设定的LLM，或可在大规模上模拟不同视角，辅助自动标注。

Method: 设计实验，评估Persona-conditioned LLM（设定不同人口学身份的模型）在三方面的表现：1）不同群体间是否产生类似人类的分歧（inter-group）；2）是否对与自身身份相关内容更敏感（in-group）；3）能否准确预测其他群体的反应（vicarious prediction），并分析多种模型和提示方式。

Result: 没有哪种模型能在这三种维度上都表现优异，表现高度依赖模型本身，简单身份设定难以自然展现这些分歧。但Llama 3.1在“代理提示”设置下，跨群体一致性和与人类分歧的相似度最高，优于其他模型和设置。

Conclusion: 当前Persona-conditioned LLM不能完全模拟人类对仇恨言论的复杂主观分歧，但合理设计身份和提示（如Llama 3.1的vicarious prompting），能更可靠地自动标注和反映人类判断模式，对实际应用有一定参考价值。

Abstract: Hate speech detection is inherently subjective: people from different demographic groups perceive the same content very differently. Collecting enough annotations from multiple demographic groups is costly and difficult to scale. Persona-conditioned Large Language Models (models prompted to adopt a specific demographic identity) have been proposed as a way to simulate diverse perspectives at scale. But do they actually reflect how different groups disagree? We evaluate three aspects of human social judgement: (i) whether personas from different groups disagree in human-like ways (inter-group disagreement), (ii) whether they become more sensitive when content targets their own identity (in-group sensitivity), and (iii) whether they can accurately predict how another group would react (vicarious prediction). Our results show that no model consistently captures all three dimensions, and performance is highly model-dependent and does not emerge reliably from minimal identity prompts alone. However, vicarious prompting with Llama 3.1 yields the highest cross-group agreement in most demographic axes and provides the closest overall approximation to human disagreement patterns, indicating that this configuration may provide a more reliable setting for automatic annotation aligned with human judgements.

### [171] [FOXGLOVE: Understanding Goal-Oriented and Anchored Writing Feedback from Experts and LLMs on Argumentative Essays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06271)
*Yijun Liu,Yifan Song,John Gallagher,Sarah Sterman,Tal August*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然LLM生成写作反馈逐渐普及，但尚无针对与专家反馈在核心写作修订维度上（目标导向、锚定具体句子、优先级排序）系统性比较的工作。本文意在填补该空白，揭示两者共性与差异。

Method: 作者构建FOXGLOVE数据集，包含专家对69篇作文的696条反馈及四个主流LLM在相同协议下生成的1644条反馈。对部分反馈进行了专家质量评级。

Result: 结果显示，专家与LLM在反馈目标和作文位置的分布上相似，但在选择具体句子、复杂度和提问数量上存在不同。LLM反馈往往更复杂、提问更少，在多数质量维度上得分更高，但主要因为篇幅更长。

Conclusion: FOXGLOVE数据集为深入比较人类与LLM作文反馈提供了基础。尽管LLM在部分维度表现优越，优势受篇幅影响较大，且与专家在关注点和表达方式上仍有差异，未来可探讨优化LLM反馈的针对性与有效性。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate writing feedback, there remains no systematic comparison of LLM and expert feedback on the dimensions that writing research identifies as central to revision: goal-orientation, anchoring to specific sentences, and prioritization. We introduce FOXGLOVE, a dataset of 696 feedback comments written by trained writing instructors on 69 twelfth-grade argumentative essays, paired with 1,644 comments generated from four frontier LLMs under a shared protocol, totaling 2,340 comments. We provide expert quality ratings on a subset of both instructor and LLM comments. We find that instructors and LLMs distribute feedback similarly across goals and essay positions, yet instructors and models diverge on the specific sentences on which to provide feedback. Additionally, we find that models tend to write more complex feedback and use fewer questions than instructors. LLM feedback also receives higher ratings on most dimensions of quality, as rated by instructors, but much of this advantage appears to be attributable to lengthier comments. FOXGLOVE enables systematic comparison of where human and LLM feedback align, diverge, and differ.

### [172] [LLMs Can Leak Training Data But Do They Want To? A Propensity-Aware Evaluation of Memorization in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06286)
*Gianluca Barmina,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出PropMe系统，区别对待大模型的攻击式与常规记忆评估，发现即使模型具备强记忆能力，普通使用时泄漏倾向普遍较低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统大模型记忆评估往往强调是否能强迫模型复现训练数据，未充分关注模型在普通使用时泄漏训练数据的概率，因此需要更全面衡量模型记忆泄漏的方法。

Method: 提出PropMe框架，对比前缀攻击和非对抗评估，提出倾向性指标变换。开发了SimpleTrace追踪工具，用于决定性归因模型生成内容，并定量分析逐字和近似泄漏。此外，在两个开源模型（Comma与DFM Decoder）、两个数据集（Common Pile与Dynaword）和两种语言上进行了实验。

Result: 实验证明，前缀攻击能显著诱发更强的记忆泄漏信号，而普通提示下模型泄漏倾向整体较低。DFM Decoder在后续训练改变数据分布后，表现出更低记忆能力和泄漏倾向。

Conclusion: 模型虽具备在特定指令下泄漏训练数据的能力，但在普通场景中风险较低。建议未来记忆泄漏评估应同时报告最坏情况和普通泄漏倾向，以便全面理解模型风险。

Abstract: Large language models can reproduce training data, but existing memorization evaluations mostly measure whether models can be forced to do so, rather than whether they do so under ordinary use. We introduce PropMe, a propensity-aware framework for memorization evaluation that contrasts prefix-based capability attacks with non-adversarial evaluations. We propose a metric transformation that, applied to existing functions, allows to create propensity metrics. We further introduce SimpleTrace, a lightweight tracing pipeline built on infini-gram that deterministically attributes model generations to large-scale training corpora and computes verbatim, near-verbatim, and propensity-transformed memorization metrics. Evaluating two fully-open models: Comma and DFM Decoder on two datasets: Common Pile and Dynaword in two languages, we find a consistent gap between capability and propensity: prefix attacks elicit substantially stronger memorization signals than generic or dataset-specific prompts, while propensity scores remain low overall. Thus, the models can reveal training data when directly elicited, but rarely do so in more common non-adversarial settings. We also find that DFM Decoder, which is continually pre-trained from Comma, exhibits reduced memorization and memorization propensity for Common Pile, confirming that memorization capability can decrease when later training emphasizes partially different data. Our results suggest, and we encourage, that memorization audits should report both worst-case extractability and ordinary leakage propensity in order to have a more comprehensive view of this phenomenon.

</details>


### [173] ["Chi nas dal soch el sent de legn" -- Auditing Text Corpora for Lombard](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06349)
*Edoardo Signoroni,Pavel Rychlý*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文分析了伦巴第语（Lombard）这一低资源语言的语料库现状，发现现有数据量虽大但噪音多且质量低，存在方言和书写系统的严重偏倚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前许多世界语言在NLP工具上仍然资源匮乏，根本原因是缺乏高质量训练和测试语料，尤其是像伦巴第语这样的低资源语言。研究动机在于了解和评估现有伦巴第语语料的数量与质量，为改进相关模型奠定基础。

Method: 作者手工审查了现有可用的平行语料和单语语料，具体分析了语料的语言识别准确性、噪声（如模板文本和非语言内容）、正字法构成（包括不同方言的书写系统及分布）。

Result: 分析发现，网络爬取语料虽大量存在，但普遍存在语言误判、噪声严重，高质量语料高度集中于西伦巴第方言，东方方言被严重忽视，不同语料间的正字法体系也不统一。

Conclusion: 现有伦巴第语语料库的数量繁荣是假象，高质量数据极度不足且代表性偏差大。未来数据建设需要关注多样性，倡导社区参与驱动的数据管理，而非单纯追求数据量。

Abstract: Several of the world's languages are still under-resourced in terms of Natural Language Processing (NLP) tools. This is mostly due to the lack of high-quality datasets to train, develop, and evaluate systems and models for several tasks, such as Machine Translation (MT). We conduct a manual audit of the parallel and monolingual corpora available for Lombard, an under-resourced language continuum from Italy. Our analysis reveals that the perceived abundance of web-scraped data is an illusion, with massive datasets plagued by severe language misidentification, boilerplate text, and non-linguistic noise. Furthermore, we analyze the orthographic composition of the valid Lombard portions across web-scraped datasets, curated corpora, and benchmarks. Our findings show conflicting orthographical systems and severe representational bias across all corpora: high-quality data is heavily skewed towards Western Lombard varieties, with Eastern ones left on the margins. This underscores the need for variety-aware, community-driven data curation rather than purely quantity-driven scraping.

</details>


### [174] [Emergent Language as an Approach to Conscious AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06380)
*Zengqing Wu,Chuan Xiao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用多智能体强化学习中涌现语言（EL）的方法来研究人工系统意识的生成机制，绕开了以往依赖于人类语言先验的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人工意识评估方法受限于理论清单或直接仿造意识模块，往往无法排除人类语言先验带来的假象。因此亟需一种剥离语言先验、直接归因于任务需求的研究范式。

Method: 提出在多智能体强化学习框架下，智能体从无语言、无自我概念、极少人类文本暴露的极小起点，通过纯粹任务压力驱动，发展出涌现通信，由此分析意识相关结构如何生成。

Result: 在一个极简环境中实验，结果发现智能体自发产生了自指通信和回声-不匹配检测机制。这些机制并非由任务结构或系统架构直接决定，而是依赖于特定环境特性自发产生。

Conclusion: 该方法绕开人类语言先验，为揭示意识相关结构的自发生成提供了新的工具和视角，有助于更深入理解人工系统意识及其前提条件。

Abstract: The question of whether artificial systems can be conscious remains open, in part because existing approaches either evaluate systems against theory-derived checklists (discriminative) or engineer consciousness-inspired modules directly (architectural); both leave open whether observed structures are artifacts of human language priors. We propose a generative methodology: emergent language (EL) in multi-agent reinforcement learning, where agents start from minimal (no language, no concept of self, minimal exposure to human text) and develop communication under task pressure alone, ensuring causal attributability to task demands rather than inherited human language priors. We position our methodology by discussing how EL serves as a generative tool for studying consciousness-relevant structure, including the role of environment complexity and the interpretation of emergent communication. As a proof of concept, we instantiate this methodology in a minimal environment and show that agents develop self-referential communication, including an echo-mismatch detection circuit that is not predicted by task structure or architecture alone but emerges from a specific environmental affordance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖继续训练或上下文中加入语法书，但容易过拟合特定语言，难以实现零样本迁移。为了规模化地翻译极低资源语言，作者认为模型应习得从上下文中提取语言知识的“元能力”。

Method: 提出用强化学习训练模型，在给定丰富语言上下文的情况下，利用表层翻译指标（chrF）作为奖励，鼓励模型提取并利用上下文中的语言信息，实现对未见语言的高效翻译。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that large language models (LLMs) can translate unseen or low-resource languages by undergoing continued training or even by encoding a grammar book in their context. However, both methods typically overfit specific languages, with limited zero-shot transfer at test time. To translate extremely low-resource languages at scale, we argue that LLMs must acquire the meta-skill of utilizing in-context linguistic knowledge rather than memorizing specific languages. In this paper, we propose a reinforcement learning (RL) approach to unseen language translation given rich linguistic context, using a surface-level translation metric (chrF) as the reward. Empirically, despite the lightweight reward, our RL-trained models effectively extract and apply relevant linguistic information from the provided context, leading to better translations on completely unseen languages than in-context learning or supervised fine-tuning. Our analyses suggest that outcome-based RL can extend beyond conventional reasoning tasks like math and coding to serve as a recipe for language learning from context.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出利用反事实对话修订作为审计LLM立场模拟的新框架。具体操作为：针对特定网聊场景，先推断目标用户对某议题的态度，再通过文本和多模态（含表情包）手段有控制地改变语境，重新模拟用户立场，并通过平均立场变动值及立场转变率量化效果。

Result: 无论是纯文本还是多模态（表情包等）语境修改，在各种立场极化和偏好机制下，均观察到有效且稳健的立场变动。模型对不同类型语境修订都出现显著的观点转变。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used to simulate social media users and infer how individuals may respond to online discussions. However, it remains unclear whether these simulations reflect precise user-specific beliefs or whether they are highly sensitive to semantically independent changes in conversational contexts. In this work, we study counterfactual context revision as a framework for auditing LLM-based stance simulation. Given an original online conversation, we first infer a target user's stance toward a specific topic. We then apply controlled revision strategies to the conversational context and simulate the user's stance again under the revised context. We compare text-only revision strategies with a multimodal one that incorporates meme-based context and evaluate two main effectiveness metrics, i.e., average directional stance shift and stance transition rate. The results reveal effective and robust stance transitions in both text-only and multimodal strategies across different polarization-preference mechanisms. Our study contributes an evaluation framework for understanding the context sensitivity of LLM-based stance simulation. More broadly, it highlights both the promise and risk of using LLMs to simulate online opinion dynamics.

### [177] [Latent Reasoning with Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06447)
*Guancheng Tu,Xiangjun Fu,Suhao Yu,Yao Tang,Haoqiang Kang,Lianhui Qin,Yizhe Zhang,Jiatao Gu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种利用normalizing flows（NF）的潜在链式思考（NF-CoT）新方法，有效结合连续状态的高带宽推理与显式链式思考（CoT）的优点，提升大语言模型推理质量并降低中间计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型中的链式思考(CoT)需要将每一步推理都转述为文本，造成推理过程离散、串行且低效。而用潜在状态进行推理虽有高带宽优势，但现有方法常损失了自回归生成、采样及高效解码等CoT优点。为兼顾CoT有效性和推理高效性，需要一种新颖的潜在推理机制。

Method: 作者提出NF-CoT框架，在语言模型内部集成TARFlow风格的normalizing flows，通过普通化流学习由显式CoT蒸馏的连续“思维”空间，连续与文本位置分别由NF头和正常LM头生成，二者共享因果自回归流。这让模型能在KV-cache支持下，概率式、从左到右地解码并直接在潜在空间进行策略梯度优化，同时获得连续“思维”的精确似然。

Result: 在代码生成基准测试上，NF-CoT相比于传统显式CoT及以往潜在推理方法，显著提升了任务通过率，并大幅降低了中间推理的计算开销。

Conclusion: NF-CoT以连续潜在思维流有机结合了CoT和高效推理的优势，为语言模型的推理效率与质量带来了实用提升，在生成等实际应用中表现更优。

Abstract: Large language models often improve reasoning by generating explicit chain-of-thought (CoT), demonstrating the importance of intermediate computation. However, textual CoT forces this computation through a discrete, serial, and communication-oriented token stream: each reasoning step must be verbalized before the model can proceed, even when the underlying update is semantic, uncertain, or only partially formed. Latent reasoning offers a higher-bandwidth alternative by performing intermediate computation in compact continuous states before committing to text. Yet existing latent-reasoning methods often sacrifice key advantages that make CoT effective in autoregressive language models, including native left-to-right generation, probabilistic sampling, compatibility with KV-cache decoding, and tractable likelihood estimation. We propose NF-CoT, a latent reasoning framework that preserves these advantages by modeling continuous thoughts with normalizing flows. NF-CoT instantiates a TARFlow-style normalizing flow inside the LLM backbone, defining a tractable probability model over compact continuous thoughts distilled from explicit CoT. Continuous-thought positions are generated by an NF head, while text positions are generated by the standard LM head within the same causal stream. This design provides exact likelihoods for latent thoughts, enables probabilistic left-to-right decoding with the original KV cache, and supports direct policy-gradient optimization in the latent reasoning space. On code-generation benchmarks, NF-CoT improves pass rates over explicit-CoT and prior latent-reasoning baselines while substantially reducing intermediate-reasoning cost.

</details>


### [178] [You Only Index Once: Cross-Layer Sparse Attention with Shared Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06467)
*Yutao Sun,Yanqi Zhang,Li Dong,Jianyong Wang,Furu Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为CLSA（cross-layer sparse attention）的新型稀疏注意力方法，在保证高质量推理的同时，大幅提升长上下文LLM的推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文LLM受限于推理效率，尤其是在推理型任务和需要生成长链式思维时。传统稀疏注意力方法要么牺牲质量换取加速（如块稀疏），要么虽然准确但加速有限（如token稀疏）。急需优化两者间的效率-质量矛盾。

Method: 基于KV-sharing（如YOCO）架构，CLSA不仅跨解码层共享KV缓存，还共享routing index。通过一次token级top-k选择，多层共同复用索引，实现高精度稀疏关注的同时，摊薄了路由计算的开销。整体优化了预填充、KV缓存存储和长上下文解码三大瓶颈。

Result: 在短上下文和超长上下文基准测试中，CLSA在保证精度的前提下，实现了最高7.6倍解码加速和17.1倍整体吞吐提升（128K context）。

Conclusion: CLSA打破了传统稀疏注意力的效率-质量权衡，为长上下文LLM提供了一种兼顾效率与精度的更完整的推理架构。

Abstract: Long-context inference in modern LLMs is increasingly constrained by decoding efficiency, especially in reasoning-heavy settings where models generate long intermediate chains of thought. Existing sparse attention methods often face a practical efficiency-quality trade-off. Structured block sparse methods typically provide stronger acceleration but incur noticeable quality loss, while token sparse methods are usually more accurate yet deliver limited end-to-end speedup because top-k routing over the full cache remains expensive. In this work, we propose cross-layer sparse attention (CLSA), which is built on top of KV-sharing architectures such as YOCO. The core idea is to share not only the KV cache across cross-decoder layers, but also the routing index. A single indexer computes token-level top-k selection once and reuses the resulting index across layers, thereby preserving the fine-grained selectivity of token sparse attention while amortizing the routing overhead. The resulting architecture improves all major inference bottlenecks jointly, including pre-filling, KV-cache storage, and long-context decoding. Experiments across short-context and long-context benchmarks show that CLSA is both accurate and efficient, achieving up to 7.6x decoding speedup and 17.1x overall throughput improvement at 128K context. These results suggest a more complete architectural solution for long-context LLMs that jointly advances model quality and inference efficiency.

</details>


### [179] [Self-Augmenting Retrieval for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06474)
*Paul Jünger,Justin Lovelace,Linxi Zhao,Dongyoung Go,Kilian Q. Weinberger*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在离散扩散语言模型中利用低置信度的中间token作为检索-增强生成（RAG）信号的新方法（SARDI），提升了多跳问答任务的效率和表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散语言模型在生成过程中会丢弃低置信度的候选token，传统方法没有充分利用这些中间信息；作者发现这些token可以作为提前检索证据的‘lookahead’信号，用于改进检索增强生成的效果。

Method: 作者提出了SARDI框架，该方法在模型生成的每一步，将当前低置信度但可能包含关键信息的token用于引导文档检索，然后将收集到的新证据作为后续去噪生成的辅助；该方法无需额外训练，对检索器无要求，并适用于所有具推理能力的扩散语言模型。

Result: 在五个多跳问答基准测试中，SARDI在不需要训练的场景下，检索增强扩散模型和自回归基线的表现均被超越，并且吞吐量最高提升8倍。

Conclusion: SARDI有效利用了扩散语言模型早期预测的低置信度token作为检索信号，在无需训练和高度兼容的前提下，大幅提升RAG任务的性能和效率，具有很强的实用意义。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion language models generate text by iteratively denoising an entire response in parallel. At each step, they predict tentative tokens for every masked position, committing the confident predictions to the output and discarding the unconfident ones. We show that the discarded tokens are in fact a useful lookahead signal for retrieval-augmented generation: even low-confidence tokens often surface salient entities early in the denoising trajectory, enabling retrieval of stronger evidence before the output is finalized. We exploit this through Self-Augmenting Retrieval for Diffusion Language Models (SARDI), a dynamic RAG framework that uses these lookahead tokens to guide retrieval during denoising. SARDI is training-free, retriever-agnostic, and applicable to any reasoning-capable discrete diffusion language model. Across five multi-hop QA benchmarks, SARDI outperforms current training-free diffusion and autoregressive retrieval baselines at up to $8\times$ higher throughput.

</details>


### [180] [Operation-Guided Progressive Human-to-AI Text Transformation Benchmark for Multi-Granularity AI-Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06481)
*Sondos Mahmoud Bsharat,Jiacheng Liu,Xiaohan Zhao,Tianjun Yao,Xinyi Shang,Yi Tang,Jiacheng Cui,Ahmed Elhagry,Salwa K. Al Khatib,Hao Li,Salman Khan,Zhiqiang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出OpAI-Bench基准，用于研究人类与AI协作编辑下，文本在多轮渐进编辑中的AI痕迹变化，以及检测方法在不同阶段的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI写作助手在实际写作和修订流程中的普及，越来越多文档是由人类与AI共同协作完成。当前的AI文本检测主要关注最终版本，忽略了文档在编辑过程中AI特征的显现和消失规律，因此需要新的评测基准来理解此过程。

Method: 作者开发了OpAI-Bench基准，针对四个内容领域，从人类写作文档出发，利用五种典型AI编辑操作和不同AI参与度，生成每个样本的九个逐步修订版本，并在文档、句子、Token/Span等多个层级保留作者信息。基准支持8种文档级、7种句子级、2种更细粒度检测器的综合评测实验。

Result: 实验表明，AI文本可检测性不仅受AI编辑比例影响，还与具体编辑操作、领域和累积修订历史相关。同时，混合作者的中间版本往往比纯人类或重度AI编辑版本更难检测，发现了先前基准未揭示的复杂检测模式。

Conclusion: OpAI-Bench为在实际多轮编辑场景下分析AI写作痕迹的可检测性和变化规律提供了受控测试平台，能够更真实地评估和推动AI文本检测方法的发展。

Abstract: As AI writing assistants become increasingly integrated into real-world drafting and revision workflows, many documents are no longer purely human-written or AI-generated, but instead result from progressive human-AI co-editing. However, existing AI-text detection benchmarks largely focus on final outputs and provide limited understanding of how AI authorship signals emerge, accumulate, or disappear throughout the revision process. We introduce OpAI-Bench, an operation-guided benchmark for studying progressive human-to-AI text transformation across document, sentence, token, and span granularities. Starting from human-written documents, OpAI-Bench constructs nine sequentially revised versions for each sample under predefined AI coverage levels and five representative AI edit operations, covering four domains while preserving complete authorship provenance at multiple granularities. The benchmark supports comprehensive evaluation with 8 document-level detectors, 7 sentence-level detectors, and 2 fine-grained token/span-level detectors. Experiments reveal that AI-text detectability is governed not only by the proportion of AI-edited content, but also by edit operation, domain, and cumulative revision history. Interestingly, we notice that mixed-authorship intermediate versions are often harder to detect than both fully human and heavily AI-edited endpoints, exposing non-monotonic detection patterns missed by existing benchmarks. OpAI-Bench provides a controlled testbed for analyzing whether, when, and how AI-assisted writing becomes detectable under realistic progressive editing scenarios. Our code and benchmark are available at https://github.com/VILA-Lab/OpAI-Bench.

</details>

### [181] [OLIVE: Online Low-Rank Incremental Learning for Efficient Adaptive Exoskeletons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05234)
*Dong Liu,Yanxuan Yu,Ben Lengerich,Tony Geng,Ying Nian Wu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可持续在线个性化的外骨骼控制框架OLIVE，通过高效低秩增量学习，实现了在真实复杂环境下对用户步态的快速自适应，大幅提升了步态平滑性、省力性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大多数外骨骼控制器使用静态步态策略，难以适应动态环境或不同个体，限制了其在真实情境下的应用效果。因此急需能够持续自适应并个性化调整的控制方法。

Method: OLIVE 框架将控制策略的自适应部分分解为低秩残差（公式：ΔW=AB^T），显著减少了在线更新参数的计算量。参数通过基于身体传感器（EMG、IMU、振动）的奖励型策略梯度自动更新，无需离线参考轨迹。框架还包含上下文门控机制和动态秩调度，根据地形复杂度灵活调整更新维度，实现既高效又鲁棒的个性化控制。

Result: 在穿戴式外骨骼平台实验表明，OLIVE在步态平滑性、省力性和动作稳定性上比最优对比基线分别提升了13、22、15个百分点，并可在约1800步内收敛，端到端延迟仅7.4ms。

Conclusion: OLIVE是高效在线个性化外骨骼控制的新范式，能够兼顾实时性和适应性，在复杂动态环境下显著提升穿戴者行走体验，为外骨骼广泛实际应用提供了有力支撑。

Abstract: Wearable exoskeleton systems hold promise for restoring mobility in individuals with physical impairments, yet most existing controllers rely on static gait policies that lack the ability to adapt to dynamic real-world environments or individual user characteristics. We present \olive (\underline{O}nline \underline{L}ow-rank \underline{I}ncremental Learning for Efficient Adapti\underline{ve} Exoskeletons), a parameter-efficient online adaptation framework that continuously personalizes exoskeleton control during deployment. \olive decomposes the adaptive component of the control policy into a low-rank residual form~$\dW = \At\Bt^\top$ with rank~$r!\ll!\min(d,k)$, reducing online update cost from $\mathcal{O}(dk)$ to $\mathcal{O}(r(d{+}k))$ while preserving the stability of a pretrained base controller~$\Wz$. Parameters are updated via a reward-shaped policy gradient driven purely by on-body sensor feedback (EMG, IMU, vibration), eliminating dependence on offline reference trajectories. A gating mechanism modulates the strength of personalization based on contextual state, and a dynamic rank scheduler adapts the update dimensionality to terrain complexity -- allocating minimal capacity on simple flat terrain and expanding to higher-rank updates on demanding uneven surfaces -- enabling robust performance across diverse activities: flat walking, stair navigation, slopes, and uneven terrain. Experiments on the wearable platform demonstrate that \olive achieves +13, +22, and +15 percentage-point improvements in gait smoothness, effort reduction, and motion stability over the strongest baseline, converging within $\sim$1{,}800 walking steps at 7.4,ms end-to-end latency. Our code implementation is available at https://github.com/FastLM/OLIVE.

</details>

Here we show a that a 4-segment, 8-joint manipulator can achieve a broader workspace than extant configurations, at lower hardware cost, and that Residual Reinforcement Learning outperforms extant state-of-the-art methods -- specifically, the FABRIK algorithm -- on the control of such manipulator. Our results show that this configuration is more workspace-effective than prior designs, and that Residual Reinforcement Learning outperforms FABRIK by three orders of magnitude on positional and orientational accuracy, effecting precise control of the novel 4-segment, 8-joint manipulator. Additionally, the control implementation is simpler: we describe the complete FABRIK process for control and corresponding learning implementation. Our methodology is applicable to the design of new systems, providing designers with further tools for the development of this class of manipulators and corresponding control systems for novel configurations.

*Yigit Yildirim,Giuseppe Rauso,Riccardo Caccavale,Alberto Finzi*

Main category: cs.RO

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的逆向机器人操作方法仅通过符号状态逆转或运动轨迹回放，难以恢复连续动力学下执行的真实结果，导致逆向计划不准确。本文旨在解决复杂交互任务中逆向恢复的不足。

Method: 首先利用从演示中自动提取的STRIPS风格操作符与几何谓词生成逆向技能目标；通过任务规划器先用已有动作原语满足逆向条件，未解决部分转为剩余操作符学习问题，采用强化学习进行补充优化。

Abstract: Inverting a robotic task requires more than reversing symbolic state transitions or rewinding motor trajectories. In robot manipulation tasks, symbolic inverse plans often fail to fully restore the effects of forward executions under continuous interaction dynamics. We present a hybrid framework for inverse manipulation that derives inverse-skill objectives from STRIPS-like operators automatically extracted from demonstrations through soft geometric predicates. For each extracted operator, we construct an inverse restoration objective that preserves preconditions, restores delete effects, and negates add effects. A task planner first attempts to satisfy this objective using available action primitives. Unresolved symbolic predicates then induce a residual operator learning problem solved through Reinforcement Learning (RL). We evaluate the framework on the ManiSkill3 PushCube task. For a forward pushing skill, the symbolic inverse performs a coarse pick-and-place restoration, while a residual Soft Actor-Critic policy refines the cube pose to satisfy the remaining inverse predicates. Our results show that predicate-derived residual control can turn an approximate symbolic inverse into a physically grounded inverse skill.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种利用G-多项式曲线结构（推广到矩阵Lie群的多项式曲线）的方法，将点到曲线的距离计算简化为少量多项式求根问题，并给出SE(3)情形的实用公式，实现包已公开。

Abstract: Vector-field-based methods are widely used for robot control and are often applied to the path-tracking problem. Some vector field approaches require repeatedly computing the distance between the robot configuration and the curve, as well as the corresponding closest point. Recently, vector fields have been extended to Lie Groups. In this case, this computation can be expensive, especially when performed at high control frequencies on embedded platforms. This paper proposes a method for efficiently computing the distance between a point and a curve represented as what is called a G-polynomial curve, which is a curve representation that generalizes polynomial curves to matrix Lie groups. The proposed approach exploits the structure of these curves to reduce the problem to a small number of polynomial root-finding computations. Simulation results show that the method significantly reduces computation time while maintaining accuracy compared to existing optimization-based approaches. Practical formulas are also provided for the case of the group SE(3), and the method is validated experimentally on a robotic manipulator. The methodology is implemented in a computational package, available online.

### [185] [VASO: Formally Verifiable Self-Evolving Skills for Physical AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05395)
*Yunhao Yang,Neel P. Bhatt,Kevin Wang,Samuel Tetteh,Zhangyang Wang,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: VASO提出了一种通过形式化验证引导大模型生成机器人格技能自进化的框架，将反例作为技能优化反馈，大幅提升机器人技能的安全性和可复用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大模型大幅降低了机器人技能的生成成本，但其在真实环境下的可靠性和安全性难以保障，现有方法多通过执行反馈、测试等提供有限的证明，不能系统性验证长期安全。作者希望构建一种机制，实现技能的自动化、自适应安全改善。

Method: VASO框架将每个机器人技能表示为语义契约，涵盖形式化接口（用于模型检测）与规划接口（生成可执行行为）。先由形式化方法验证技能及其生成的行为是否符合集体/局部时序安全约束。若不满足安全要求，用形式化反例生成“文本梯度”反馈，驱动技能契约更新，但保持基础大模型权重不变。

Result: 在Clearpath Jackal和PX4无人机任务上，VASO达到97.2%的形式规范合规性，用于优化采样次数少于100次，显著优于传统的执行反馈、提示优化和微调等方法。

Conclusion: VASO首次实现了形式化验证与大模型生成技能的闭环自进化，能将安全反例直接转化为技能契约的优化信号，提升了物理机器人智能体的可靠性和安全性，推动了可复用机器人技能的发展。

Abstract: Reusable robot skills are becoming the basic units through which embodied agents turn open-ended instructions into long-horizon physical behavior. We argue that, while foundation models have collapsed the cost of creating these skills, the cost of trusting them has not. Existing skill-evolution loops refine skills through execution feedback, unit tests, environment reward, or LLM self-critique, but these signals provide only trace-level evidence: they show that a skill worked on sampled executions, not that skill-induced plans satisfy temporal safety contracts under untested conditions. We introduce VASO, a framework for verification-guided self-evolution of LLM-generated robot skill contracts. In VASO, each skill is represented as a semantic contract with two coupled interfaces: a formal interface that aligns robot states, observations, and control commands with logical propositions for model checking, and a planner-facing interface that guides executable behavior generation. A model checker first filters logically inconsistent skill contracts, then verifies plans induced by the skill against global and local temporal specifications. When verification fails, VASO translates the counterexample trace into a textual gradient that updates the reusable skill contract while keeping foundation-model weights frozen. On Clearpath Jackal and PX4 quadcopter tasks, VASO reaches 97.2% formal-specification compliance using fewer than 100 optimization samples, outperforming execution-feedback, prompt-optimization, and fine-tuning baselines. To our knowledge, VASO is the first framework that closes the loop between formal verification and self-evolving LLM-generated skills for physical AI agents: formal counterexamples become optimization feedback for reusable robot skill contracts, rather than merely verifying one-off plans, tuning planner prompts, or fine-tuning model weights.

</details>


### [186] [MoDex: A Diffusion Policy for Sequential Multi-Object Dexterous Grasping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05407)
*Haofei Lu,Hongjia Liu,Yifei Dong,Florian T. Pokorny,Jens Lundell,Danica Kragic*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的多物体顺序抓取方法MoDex，能让单手灵巧机械手在保持已抓物体不放的前提下继续抓取新物体，并在仿真和现实实验中取得了比现有方法更高的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的灵巧抓取方法通常把全部自由度分配给单一目标物体，导致机械手抓取多个物体时无法利用其全部灵活性。本研究旨在探索如何让机械手有效地顺序抓取多个物体，同时保留部分自由度用于后续操作。

Method: 提出了MoDex方法，采用扩散策略(Diffusion Policy)直接根据观测预测下一个抓手姿态。核心做法是引入对抗空间(opposition space)条件，指定参与当前抓取的手指子集，从而只用部分自由度进行操作，预留其余自由度用于下一次抓取。采用先模仿学习（利用专家演示）、再强化学习微调的两阶段训练策略，以提升仿真到现实的迁移效果。

Result: 在MuJoCo仿真平台和真实的Franka Emika Panda机器人加Allegro Hand硬件上验证了方法有效性。实验表明，MoDex在仿真和现实两种环境下，抓取成功率分别比现有学习方法高2.92-17.92%及6.67-17.78%。

Conclusion: MoDex充分利用机械手的冗余自由度，实现了无需释放已抓取物体的多物体顺序抓取，且在仿真和现实都显著优于现有学习方法，对提高灵巧手多任务操作能力具有实际意义。

Abstract: This work addresses sequentially grasping multiple objects with a single dexterous hand without releasing those already held. Most dexterous grasping methods commit all of the hand's degrees of freedom to a single object, underutilizing its dexterity and leaving no redundancy for subsequent grasps. The proposed solution, MoDex, is a diffusion policy that predicts the next gripper pose directly from observations, conditioned on an opposition space and point cloud. The opposition space condition specifies which fingers participate in the current grasp, enabling the gripper to use only a subset of its available degrees of freedom while reserving the remaining degrees of freedom for subsequent grasps. To facilitate sim-to-real transfer, MoDex is trained in two stages: first through imitation learning on expert demonstrations, and subsequently through reinforcement learning fine-tuning, which consistently improves success rates over the pre-trained policy. We evaluate MoDex in simulation on a MuJoCo-based Franka Emika Panda robot equipped with an Allegro Hand and on the corresponding real-world hardware platform. Across both simulation and real-world experiments, MoDex achieves higher success rates than the evaluated learning-based baselines, improving performance by 2.92-17.92% and 6.67-17.78%, respectively. Project page: https://modex2026.github.io/.

</details>

Abstract: Learning from demonstratins (LfD) is usually performed over Euclidean spaces, while the robot state, e.g. orientation, naturally evolves over curved spaces. Here, geodesic paths provide for natural motion between two arbitrary points within the manifold. We propose to numerically estimate geodesics via neural ordinary differential equations, mitigating large computational overhead of existing approaches. Finally, these geodesics can be decoded back into the original task space before deploying on the robot. ### [189] [FlowPRO: Reward-Free Reinforced Fine-Tuning of Flow-Matching VLAs via Proximalized Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05468)
*Yihao Wu,He Zhang,Junbo Tan,Xueqian Wang,Zhengyou Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA模型向可真实部署的机器人策略转化时面临很大瓶颈，现有方法（如SFT、DAgger、基于奖励的RL等）存在失败信号利用方式间接、奖励设计难、批评器训练难等问题，亟需能更高效、直接提升策略性能的新方法。

Method: 提出FlowPRO框架及其优化目标RPRO（Robotic Flow-matching Proximalized Preference Optimization），结合了对比优化器和显式邻近正则项，避免原有方法的奖励黑客化问题。在数据采集上提出用遥操作生成正反案例轨迹，并通过插值和批量混合，转换为更密集的逐状态监督。

Abstract: Post-training Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models into policies that can be reliably deployed on real robots remains a major bottleneck. SFT and DAgger exploit failure signals only indirectly, and reward-based RL is bottlenecked by the difficulty of real-world reward design and of training reliable critics. We present FlowPRO, a reward-free offline reinforced fine-tuning framework for flow-matching VLAs. Algorithmically, we propose RPRO (Robotic Flow-matching Proximalized Preference Optimization), a preference-optimization objective tailored to the flow-matching action head of VLA models. RPRO pairs a contrastive optimizer with an explicit proximal regularizer that anchors the absolute magnitude of the implicit reward, thereby eliminating the reward-hacking failure mode of plain Flow-DPO. On the data side, a teleoperated intervention-and-rollback paradigm produces naturally paired positive and negative trajectories $(τ^w, τ^l)$ on a real robot from a single operator action; a Smooth Interpolation procedure, combined with batch mixing, then converts these sparse corrections into dense per-state supervision while preserving the base policy's capabilities. On four long-horizon bimanual tasks, FlowPRO attains the highest success rate, outperforming four representative baselines, and ablations confirm the contribution of each loss component.

Motivation: 足式机器人里，足端速率为零的假设是里程计估算的基础，需要准确检测落地（支撑）和摆动相，常用的力传感器并非所有机器人都具备，且容易对地面滑移等异常不敏感。

Result: 实验结果显示，该自监督检测器在无需更多标签和传感器的情况下，效果优于有监督方法和传统概率法。

Conclusion: 新方法能更好地检测足式机器人步态，减少对额外硬件的要求，同时公开了相关代码，促进后续研究。

Abstract: The estimation of odometry in legged robots depends on the assumption that the velocity of the foot with respect to the world remains zero during the stance phase. Feedback for the main body velocity is derived from the kinematic serial chain of the feet making accurate leg phase detection is a critical subproblem. A considerable number of studies employ ground reaction force sensors mounted at the tip of the foot to classify, yet these sensors may not be universally available for all legged robots. Additionally, these sensors are often unresponsive to unaccounted disturbances, such as slippage, while the foot remains in contact with the ground. In this study, we propose a self-supervised representation learning framework for contact detection that utilizes the standard sensor set of joint encoders without reliance on force sensor augmentations. We employ learned representations to model the stance and swing phases probabilistically. The experimental results obtained confirm the efficacy of the proposed self-supervised contact detector. Our framework exhibited superior performance in comparison to supervised methods which necessitate sensor set augmentation and labeling, as well as baseline probabilistic approaches. Additionally, we make our code available to the public.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着体现在物理环境中的AI系统能力增强，其在实际环境中的安全问题愈发突出，尤其是长时机器人操作任务中，任何失误都可能对人、物或工作场所造成损害，因此亟需系统梳理该领域的安全研究进展与挑战。

Method: 本文采用系统性文献回顾的方法，从干预环节（包括规划时、策略执行时和运行时）对相关研究进行分类，并分析各类措施提供的安全证据类型（正式保障、统计支持、经验启发）及其局限。

Result: 结果显示，现有文献在政策设计阶段的安全证据有限，针对涉及大量接触风险的长时操作缺乏强有力的形式化安全保证，不确定性触发干预机制尚不成熟，且缺乏面向具体操作任务的安全基准测试。此外，当前的安全性支持多为间接证据。

Conclusion: 作者提出，应加强跨层安全保障、完善评测设计并推动机器人长时操作体现在现实场景中的安全部署，填补现有方法和标准化工具中的空白。

Abstract: Embodied AI systems are increasingly expected to reason and act over extended horizons in physical environments. This growing capability brings safety to the foreground, because failures in the physical world can harm people, damage objects, and disrupt workplaces. Although safe embodied AI has attracted substantial attention, the literature remains fragmented across planning, policy design, and runtime execution. Long-horizon robotic manipulation is a particularly revealing anchor domain for this problem because semantic misgrounding, subtask-level error propagation, execution drift, and contact-rich physical risk can accumulate within the same closed-loop system. This survey therefore provides a structured review of safety in long-horizon robotic manipulation from an embodied AI perspective. We organize the literature by intervention locus, covering planning-time, policy-time, and execution-time safety, and we analyze the strength of the evidence that each line of work provides, distinguishing formal guarantees, statistical support, and empirical safety heuristics. This framework clarifies the distinct roles of backbone capability papers, direct safety mechanisms, and benchmark or evaluation studies, while exposing where current safety claims are well supported and where they remain indirect. We identify persistent gaps, including limited evidence for policy-time safety, weak formal support for contact-rich long-horizon manipulation, immature uncertainty-triggered intervention, and a shortage of manipulation-specific safety benchmarks. We conclude by outlining research directions for cross-layer assurance, evaluation design, and safer deployment of long-horizon robotic agents in real-world settings.

### [193] [Preserving Full 6-DOF Actuation Under Abrupt Total Rotor Failures: Passive Fault-Tolerant Flight Control Using a Biaxial-Tilt Hexacopter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05663)
*Yipeng Yang,Yiqiao Tang,Hao Zhang,Jinqi Jiang,Jianfeng He,Rumo Chen,Xinghu Yu,Zhan Li,Huijun Gao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种双轴倾斜过驱动六旋翼无人机（BTO），能够在不依赖故障检测的情况下，应对突然的多电机失效，实现被动容错飞行。相关控制方法通过仿真和实飞实验验证，比传统结构具有更强的恢复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常规多旋翼在遭遇突发电机总失效时，失去可信的六自由度控制能力，难以保障飞行安全。因此，开发在缺乏先验故障信息时仍能保持飞行稳定的无人机架构和控制方法具有重要现实意义。

Method: 该研究扩展了AWS（可用力扭空间）的测度，综合瞬时扭力跳变分析，在最多三电机失效情况下评估BTO与传统设计的性能。提出两种高效无故障检测的被动容错方案：一是在控制器层结合高阶全驱控制器与线性扩展状态观测器以鲁棒抑制干扰；二是在分配器层利用模型参考自适应分配和基于动量的力估算补偿分配偏差。

Conclusion: BTO架构及其相应的无检测被动容错控制方法，在单/多电机失效和复杂环境下均实现了鲁棒的六自由度控制，显著提高了旋翼无人机的可靠性和可操作性。

Abstract: Conventional multirotors suffer from a rapid collapse of attainable wrench space (AWS) under abrupt total rotor failures, rendering full 6-DOF recovery physically impossible. This paper addresses passive fault-tolerant flight of a biaxial-tilt overactuated hexacopter (BTO) under abrupt total rotor failures that are a priori unknown to the controller. The control design and analysis focus on representative abrupt rotor-failure cases for which the post-failure system remains fully actuated, while no explicit fault detection, isolation, or fault-mode switching is assumed. First, we extend the inscribed-sphere metric of the AWS by incorporating the transient-wrench-jump term, enabling quantitative feasibility assessment under up to three simultaneous rotor failures and benchmarking against uniaxial-tilt and coplanar hexacopters. Second, we develop two computationally efficient passive schemes without relying on fault detection or online optimization. One scheme operates at the controller layer by combining a high-order fully actuated (HOFA) controller with a linear extended state observer (LESO) for lumped-disturbance rejection. The other scheme operates at the allocator layer by using model-reference adaptive control allocation with momentum-based wrench estimation to compensate for control-allocation biases. Simulations and flight experiments validate stable hovering and 6-DOF trajectory tracking under single and multiple rotor failures. Further systematic comparisons confirm that the BTO provides larger recovery margins than uniaxial-tilt and coplanar designs. Additional onboard-sensor-only experiments, including indoor tracking under wind disturbance, outdoor tracking under extreme conditions, narrow-frame traversal, and contact-based aerial writing, further validate the robustness of the proposed framework in complex operational environments.

Method: 提出了基于token passing(令牌传递)范式的两种事件驱动在线重规划算法：1）Dynamic Token Passing，对订单变更进行局部重规划，采用添加-订单分解及优先级令牌调度，确保避碰；2）Cooperative Token Passing，允许空闲机器人协助新增任务，提高整体效率。

Abstract: Robotic Cellular Warehousing Systems (RCWS) give rise to multi-agent pickup and delivery (MAPD) processes in which robots sequentially collect multiple stock-keeping units (SKUs) for each order. Unlike classical MAPD formulations that assume static tasks, real warehouse operations often involve dynamic order evolution, where new SKUs may be appended to an order while it is being executed. Motivated by this practical requirement, this letter formulates the Dynamic Multi-Agent Pickup and Delivery problem considering internal order evolution for the first time. Building on the token passing paradigm, we propose two event-triggered online replanning algorithms. The first, Dynamic Token Passing, performs localized replanning upon order updates through add-order decomposition and priority-based token scheduling while preserving collision-free execution. The second, Cooperative Token Passing, further enables idle robots to opportunistically assist newly added pickups, improving system-level efficiency. Simulation results in RCWS environments demonstrate that the proposed methods significantly reduce order flowtime compared with static and non-cooperative baselines.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人进行双手工具操作时高自由度控制和复杂动力学难题，现有方法依赖示范参考或高昂的规划计算，难以高效生成未来动作轨迹。

Method: 提出分层DexFuture架构，高层为视运动未来状态目标预测器，用Transformer生成多步目标轨迹；低层为目标条件化的精细控制策略，负责具体动作跟踪，实现粗-细粒度的分离控制。

Abstract: Bimanual dexterous tool use remains challenging for robots due to high-dimensional hand configurations and complex hand-tool-object dynamics and contact. Most existing control policies depend on future configuration references provided from demonstrations, while future action-conditioned world models require slow online planning over high-dimensional action sequences. A significant challenge is generating a dynamically consistent future reference trajectory without relying on privileged states from demonstrations or slow counterfactual planning. We propose DexFuture, a hierarchical system that couples a high-level Future-State Visuomotor Target Predictor with a low-level Target-Conditioned Structured Dexterous Policy. Conditioned on egocentric RGB, proprioceptive and geometric history, the high-level predictor constructs structured hand-tool-object visuomotor embeddings and uses a horizon-conditioned transformer to generate a multi-step future target trajectory. Then, the low-level policy tracks them with a target-conditioned per-link transformer. This hierarchy decouples coarse future reference generation from fine-grained action control, and slow long-horizon semantic prediction from high-frequency execution. On OakInk2 bimanual tool-use tasks, DexFuture achieves 90% of the privileged-oracle performance, compared to 7% for a no-reference policy. DexFuture operates at 60 Hz, approximately 250 times faster than DexWM-style Cross-Entropy Method (CEM) planning with a future action-conditioned world model.

### [197] [PiL-World: A Chunk-Wise World Model for VLA Policy-in-the-Loop Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05773)
*Chong Ma,Taiyi Su,Jian Zhu,Jianjun Zhang,Zitai Huang,Yi Xu,Hanli Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出PiL-World模型，实现了机器人在视觉-语言-动作任务中的闭环（closed-loop）世界模型评估，显著提高模拟和真实执行之间的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器人世界模型大多只支持在预采集的动作轨迹上做开环（open-loop）预测，无法评估每一步都依赖前一次执行结果的闭环视觉-语言-动作策略。这严重限制了无需实际机器人执行的策略验证与改进能力。

Method: 作者提出PiL-World，一种支持policy-in-the-loop闭环评估的世界模型。其主要做法是，在给定当前观测和VLA策略执行的动作轨迹下，生成符合策略需求并与实际执行一致的多视角未来观测图像。方法上通过联合学习多视角预测、融合基于动作的视频生成控制和历史执行上下文，有效提升了生成结果的真实性。此外，模型还学习失败的轨迹，增加了对真实策略分布的拟合能力。

Result: 在三个实际双臂操作任务上实验，PiL-World能够生成高度真实、与真实机器人执行极为一致的模拟轨迹。与基线方法比，使用PiL-World后，通过世界模型模拟评估的成功率与真实执行测得成功率之差由63.2%降低至12%。

Conclusion: PiL-World为机器人视觉-语言-动作策略的闭环高保真评估提供了有效解决方案，大大缩小了模拟与现实中的策略表现差距，有望显著加快复杂机器人任务的策略验证和优化进程。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) policies operate in a closed loop in real-world robot tasks: a robot observes the scene, executes an action chunk, and conditions its next decision on the resulting observation. However, most existing world models for robot action evaluation are limited to open-loop prediction along pre-collected action trajectories. This prevents them from supporting closed-loop VLA evaluation, where each action chunk must be conditioned on the observation generated by the previous execution. To address this gap, we propose PiL-World, a chunk-wise world model designed for policy-in-the-loop VLA evaluation. Given the current observation and the action trajectory rolled out by a VLA policy, PiL-World generates multi-view future observations that are consistent with the VLA rollout and match the image inputs required by the policy. By alternating between VLA inference and world-model prediction, PiL-World enables closed-loop evaluation without real robot execution at every step. To improve rollout fidelity, PiL-World conditions video generation on action-derived visual control from head-view robot motion and latent histories that encode task execution context, while jointly predicting complementary multi-view observations. Beyond successful teleoperated demonstrations, it also learns from failed execution trajectories, helping the imagined rollouts better match the distribution of real policy executions. We evaluate PiL-World on three real dual-arm manipulation tasks. PiL-World generates imagined rollouts that are highly consistent with real robot executions. More importantly, compared with the baseline, it reduces the error between VLA success rates measured in real-world rollouts and those estimated through closed-loop world-model evaluation from 63.2% to 12.0%.

### [198] [Visuotactile and Explicitly Force-Controlled Robotic Ultrasound for Abdominal Volumetric Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05848)

Abstract: In this paper, we present a robotic ultrasound acquisition system that integrates stereo vision, touch-based feedback, and expert-informed strategies to perform autonomous and adaptive abdominal scans. Using stereo vision, the system generates three-dimensional topography maps of the patient's abdomen, which are refined through stiffness measurements at key points to delineate the rib cage boundary. These combined techniques enable the robot to execute two distinct scanning paths: an upward-angled sweep beneath the rib cage to visualize structures near the upper abdomen and a perpendicular sweep across soft tissue regions. A compliant, torque-controlled seven degree-of-freedom robotic manipulator is controlled to maintain consistent probe contact through closed-loop force control over the varied anatomical surfaces. Physical experiments demonstrate that the system achieves high-quality imaging comparable to expert scans while dynamically adapting to patient-specific topographies. Furthermore, the robotic system surpasses expert capabilities by enabling three-dimensional volume acquisition, which enhances diagnostic potential and provides volumetric data for advanced analyses. This work highlights the integration of expert knowledge into autonomous robotic systems and underscores the potential of combining perception-based autonomy with physical reasoning for enhanced diagnostic performance.

</details>


### [199] [LadderMan: Learning Humanoid Perceptive Ladder Climbing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05873)
*Siheng Zhao,Yuanhang Zhang,Ziqi Lu,Pieter Abbeel,Rocky Duan,Koushil Sreenath,Yue Wang,C. Karen Liu,Guanya Shi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了LadderMan系统，使类人机器人能够在各种梯形环境中稳定攀爬并进行操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 攀爬梯子对于类人机器人来说极具挑战性，因其脚手点稀疏、全身协调复杂、对感知和控制误差敏感。目前缺乏可泛化且能应对实物环境的类人机器人爬梯解决方案。

Method: 提出一个分两阶段的学习流程，首先用混合动作跟踪从单一参考动作中学习多个攀爬专家技能，再通过模仿与强化学习融合，将多个专家技能提炼成统一的、基于深度视觉的视觉-运动攀爬策略，并借助视觉基础大模型提升从仿真到真实的深度感知泛化能力。此外，还构建了一个双代理模型，实现在梯子上通过远程操控完成操作任务。

Result: LadderMan系统在各种梯子几何结构下都能实现鲁棒的攀爬，并能零样本迁移到真实硬件，在梯子约束下支持多种操作任务。

Conclusion: LadderMan系统为解决类人机器人在实际人类环境中爬梯及操作任务的挑战提供了有效解决方案，显著提升了类人机器人在复杂环境下的自主能力。

Abstract: Humanoid robots hold great promise for operating in human-centered environments, yet ladder climbing remains one of the most challenging tasks due to sparse footholds and handholds, complex whole-body coordination, and sensitivity to perception and control errors. We present \textbf{LadderMan}, a unified system that enables humanoid robots to robustly climb diverse ladders and perform manipulation under such constrained conditions. Our climbing policy is built on a scalable two-stage learning pipeline, where we use hybrid motion tracking to learn multiple climbing experts from a single reference motion, and distill these experts into a unified depth-based visuomotor climbing policy via hybrid imitation and reinforcement learning. To enable real-world deployment, we leverage vision foundation models to bridge the sim-to-real gap in depth perception. Building on the learned climbing policy, we further train a separate manipulation policy using a dual-agent formulation, allowing stable on-ladder manipulation via teleoperation. Experiments demonstrate that LadderMan achieves robust ladder climbing across a wide range of geometries, successfully transfers to real-world hardware in a zero-shot manner, and supports various manipulation tasks under challenging ladder constraints. Video results are available at https://ladderman-robot.github.io .

### [200] [TAGA: Terrain-aware Active Gaze Learning for Generalizable Agile Humanoid Locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05880)
*Peizhuo Li,Hongyi Li,Mingfeng Fan,Fangzhou Xu,Shuhao Liao,Yuxuan Ma,Zicheng Zeng,Ze Wang,Yongbin Jin,Yuhong Cao,Hongtao Wang,Guillaume Sartoretti*

TL;DR: 该论文提出TAGA，一种面向地形感知的主动凝视学习框架，使仿人机器人能在复杂多变地形上实现高效、稳定的灵巧行走。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 灵巧的仿人机器人行走需要兼顾广泛的感知覆盖和对局部地形的精确理解。受到人类在行走时有选择性观察地形的启发，旨在提升机器人对地形的适应性与感知效率。

Method: 提出TAGA框架，将视觉、运动感知和运动指令进行融合，让模型通过强化学习自主学习预测地形信息，并主动聚焦于高度扫描中的关键区域，在有限计算资源下提升观察信息密度。

Result: 强化学习下无需显式监督即可自然学得有效的凝视行为，显著提高训练效率。所训练出的策略在仿真与实际硬件均表现出强健的地形感知行走能力，包括可靠的落足点选择、高台跨越、稀疏落足点和1.2m大间隙跨越，是同类系统最大真实跨越距离。

Conclusion: TAGA方法能在有限感知和算力下，使仿人机器人在复杂地形下实现稳定、高效且具有泛化性的灵巧行走，推动感知驱动机器人运动控制发展。

Abstract: Agile humanoid locomotion across diverse challenging terrain demands both wide perceptual coverage and precise local geometry understanding. Motivated by the way humans selectively look at relevant terrain during locomotion, we introduce TAGA, a Terrain-aware Active Gaze learning framework for Attention-based humanoid control. By fusing vision, proprioception, and motion commands, our framework guides the model to learn anticipatory cues and actively attend to specific areas of the height scan, selectively using these informative regions for the downstream network. This adaptively increases the information density of observations under tight onboard computational constraints, thus enabling fine-grained perceptive locomotion over larger-scale terrains. We find that such gaze behaviors can naturally emerge through reinforcement learning alone, without requiring additional supervision or explicit guidance, significantly improve training efficiency. As a result, the trained policy demonstrates robust and generalizable locomotion in simulation and on hardware, including reliable terrain-aware foothold selection, elevated-platform traversal, competitive sparse-foothold traversal, and the largest reported real-world gap traversal distance of 1.2m among perceptive humanoid locomotion systems, while maintaining stability under severe perceptual disturbances and environmental interference.

### [201] [A Novel Method with Encoder-Decoder for Cross-Sensor Adaptation in Surface Shape Sensing with Sparse Strain Sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05903)
*Shuo Wang,Heng Luo,Dian Jin,Xiaoming Tao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 传感器阵列因自身或安装造成性能差异，导致形状感知不一致。该文提出结合元学习和小样本自适应的编码器-解码器网络，实现跨传感器阵列高效适应并极大降低误差和训练成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法需要针对每个传感器阵列单独训练模型，数据和时间成本高，且容易产生误差，限制了实际应用价值。该研究意图解决跨传感器阵列适应难、效率低的问题。

Method: 提出了一种结合元学习和少样本自适应的编码器-解码器神经网络结构，用于稀疏应变传感器阵列表面形状感知，实现不同传感器阵列间的快速模型迁移和适应。

Result: 实验表明，利用该方法新部署的传感器阵列只需少量新标注数据（<5%）和极短的自适应时间（<1秒）即可将感知误差从23mm降至约4mm；误差低于5mm的数据点数提升超过65%。

Conclusion: 该方法显著降低了形状感知中的训练和数据负担，提升了跨传感器阵列泛化能力，具有在软体机器人和可穿戴设备等领域的广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Performance variations in sensor arrays, caused by intrinsic differences or installation conditions, can lead to inconsistent results during shape sensing. To obtain accurate results, a large amount of data is usually required, and a separate model must be retrained for each sensor array, thereby increasing the cost and time of data acquisition, transmission, and computation. To address this issue, this work proposes an encoder-decoder architecture for surface shape sensing based on sparse strain sensors and further incorporates meta-learning and few-shot adaptation strategies to enable adaptation across different groups of sensor arrays. Experimental results demonstrate that, after the cross-sensor adaptation, a newly deployed sensor array achieves a sensing error of approximately 4.0 mm relying on less than 5.0% newly labeled data and requiring an adaptation time of under 1 second, which represents a substantial improvement from 23.0 mm error without adaptation and 20-minute data collection time required to train a new model. Moreover, the number of points with errors below 5.0 mm increased by more than 65.0%. These results indicate that the proposed method can substantially reduce the cost and training burden of surface shape sensing, and it has broad potential applications in soft robotics and wearable devices.

Method: 将场景生成建模为Red Team（红队）和Blue Team（蓝队）之间的对抗博弈。Red Team负责生成潜在失效的危险场景，Blue Team则不断改进安全策略以应对这些危险。博弈迭代过程中结合传统风险建模、对抗生成与现代学习方法，实现困难危险情形的高效发掘与策略提升。

Conclusion: 通过将风险建模、对抗生成和机器学习整合为博弈化自动训练框架，本文为物理AI系统安全嵌入提出了新思路，有望推动机器人等自动化系统在现实环境中更安全可靠地运行。

Abstract: In this work, we propose an agentic gamification framework for hazard-informed learning of robot safety policies through synthetic scenarios. We model scenario generation as an adversarial game between two agents: a Red Team that explores the space of potential failures by constructing hazardous situations, and a Blue Team that incrementally refines safety policies to prevent them. This iterative process enables efficient discovery of high-risk edge cases that are unlikely to be captured through random simulation or manual enumeration. By combining classical risk modeling with adversarial scenario generation and modern learning paradigms, this work provides a scalable pathway for embedding safety into Physical AI systems operating in complex real-world environments. The paper describes ongoing work. The contribution is a problem formulation and a proposed solution architecture.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 基于World Model的数据飞轮框架为工业具身智能系统的数据驱动、闭环优化提供了新思路，可有效提升策略学习的覆盖面、鲁棒性及持续性能，具备推广至更广泛工业场景的潜力。

Abstract: Embodied intelligence is moving from laboratory demonstrations toward industrial deployment, with the logistics industry serving as a key application scenario. Learning-based policies offer a promising path beyond traditional perception-planning-control pipelines, but their scalability depends on how embodied data can be collected, organized, and reused. This research studies a data-centric framework for industrial embodied intelligence by constructing a logistics data flywheel. Our framework converts daily operations into reusable data assets, uses World Models to generate reliable supervision for long-tail parcel manipulation, and feeds deployment feedback back into policy improvement. As an initial result, \textit{WM-DAgger} introduces a World-Model-based data aggregation framework that synthesizes out-of-distribution recovery data for robust imitation learning. Building on this result, ongoing work explores how large-scale in-the-wild multimodal data, including labeled human demonstrations, unlabeled operational videos, and system-level robot logs, can be aligned for policy learning and transformed into feedback for continual system improvement.

### [204] [World-Language-Action Model for Unified World Modeling, Language Reasoning, and Action Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05979)
*Yi Yang,Zhihong Liu,Siqi Kou,Yiyang Chen,Yanzhe Hu,Jianbo Zhou,Boyuan Zhao,Zhijie Wei,Xiao Xia,Xueqi Li,Pengfei Liu,Zhijie Deng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了世界-语言-行动（WLA）模型，一种新型的具身基础模型，能联合处理文本、图像和机器人状态，多模态预测子任务、子目标与机器人动作，并在多任务及长时序任务中取得了新状态水平的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的具身基础模型在学习世界环境建模和复杂推理执行长时序任务上各具优势但分属不同模型，难以兼顾强大的世界模型学习与语言推理能力，因此作者希望设计一个能同时融合两者优点的新架构以提升机器人跨任务泛化与执行能力。

Method: WLA模型以自回归Transformer为主干，输入文本指令、图像和机器人状态，联合预测下一个语义意图、目标图片与物理动力学。借助世界专家的监督优化物理动力，配合动作专家利用物理知识刻画状态-动作关联；通过meta-query使世界预测隐式影响动作生成，推理时可关闭或激活世界预测从而在无需世界模型时也能高效推理，支持推理测试时可扩展性。

Result: WLA-0原型（20亿参数）在NVIDIA RTX 5090上推理延迟仅40毫秒。实测在RoboTwin2.0 Clean多任务场景达到92.94%成功率，在RMBench复杂任务集下达56.5%，超越现有同类方法。且可仅用不同机器人视频直接学习新任务，无需动作注释。

Conclusion: WLA模型高效融合世界建模与语言推理能力，实现了多模态输入下机器人跨任务、长时序学习的突破，提升了实际部署中的灵活性与可扩展性，为机器人学习与泛化能力开拓了新方向。

Abstract: We propose world-language-action (WLA) models as a new class of embodied foundation models. WLA takes textual instructions, images, and robot states as inputs to jointly predict textual subtasks, subgoal images, and robot actions, conjoining the \emph{world modeling interface} to learn from extensive egocentric videos as in the world-action model (WAM) and the \emph{language reasoning} capacities to solve complex long-horizon tasks as in vision-language-action (VLA) models. At the core of WLA lies an \emph{autoregressive (AR)} Transformer backbone, instead of a bidirectional diffusion Transformer as in WAMs, to predict the \emph{next state}, comprising the \emph{semantic-level} textual intention and complementary \emph{fine-grained} physical dynamics. The physical dynamics are supervised by the world modeling objective based on a dedicated World Expert, and are leveraged to ease the characterization of the state-action correlation for the Action Expert. WLA leverages meta-queries to make the world prediction \emph{implicitly} impact the action generation so that the former can be disabled during inference. The world prediction can also be activated to enable test-time scaling for improved robot control. Our WLA-0 prototype, with 2B active parameters, achieves 40 ms per inference on an NVIDIA RTX 5090. Evaluations across simulated and real-world environments demonstrate that WLA-0 achieves state-of-the-art multi-task and long-horizon learning abilities, e.g., 92.94\% success rate on RoboTwin2.0 Clean and 56.5\% success rate on RMBench. WLA-0 also holds the promise to learn novel tasks directly from \emph{cross-embodiment robot videos} without action annotations.
